add_namespace = ww1_xinhai
add_namespace = ww1_china



###################################################

# XINHAI REVOLUTION

# GUANGZHOU UPRISING
#######################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_xinhai.1.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_guangzhou_uprising
	id = ww1_xinhai.1
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_global_flag = guangzhou_uprising
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = CHI_xinhai_revolution_mission
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = CHI_xinhai_revolution_mission
				days = -100
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.10
				days = 17
			}
		}
	}
}

# XINHAI REVOLUTION STARTS
#############################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_xinhai.2.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_wuchang_revolt
	id = ww1_xinhai.2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_lu_rongting = {
				set_nationality = CHI
			}
			
			CHI = {
				inherit_technology = QIN
				
				set_temp_variable = { CHI_tempvar_rebellion_province = 5 }
				
			
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_hubei
				set_state_owner = 620
				set_province_controller = 4619
				set_province_controller = 7167
				set_province_controller = 12467
				
				
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = QIN
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = TAN
							region = 146
							state = 330
							state = 982
							state = 983
						}
					}
					add_core_of = CHI
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = QIN
					}
					add_claim_by = CHI
				}
				
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
					long_name = CHI_hubei_party
					name = CHI_hubei_party
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 5
					communism = 0
					democratic = 36
					neutrality = 59
				}
				promote_character = CHI_li_yuanhong
				
				
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = china_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				copy_unequal_treaties_ideas = yes
				# Prevents early surrender
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = CHI_idea_revolutionary_fervor
					days = 30 # Maximum time for second revolt to happen: 30 days
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = QIN_idea_xinhai_revolution
					days = 125
				}
			}
			

			CHI = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = QIN
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = QIN
				load_oob = "PRC_1911_Wuchang"
				
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_xinhai_revolution
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -1.0
			}
			#set_global_flag = QIN_next_uprising
			# clr_global_flag = wuchang_uprising
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.15 #Jingzhou
						days = 3
						random_days = 2
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.12 #Hunan
						days = 5
						random_days = 2
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
			
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.13 #Shaanxi
						days = 5
						random_days = 2
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.14 #Jiangxi
						days = 8
						random_days = 2
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.16 #Shanxi
						days = 10
						random_days = 2
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.17 #Shanghai --- SETS COSMETIC FLAG
						days = 12
						random_days = 3
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.18 #Yunnan/Guizhou
						days = 10
						random_days = 5
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.19 #Zhejiang
						days = 20
						random_days = 6
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.20 #Guangxi
						days = 15
						random_days = 5
						random_hours = 5
					}
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.21 #Sichuan
						days = 40
						random_days = 15
						random_hours = 7
					}
				
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_xinhai.22 #Shandong
						days = 30
						random_days = 10
						random_hours = 9
					}
				}
			}
			
			CHI = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai } }
					add_named_threat = {
						threat = 5
						name = ww1_xinhai.2.t
					}
					set_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Support Qing
		name = ww1_xinhai.2.a
		news_event = { id = kis_news.107 hours = 3 	}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.35
			}
			#reformats
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = QIN_reform_association_long
				name = QIN_reform_association
			}
			# QIN = {
			# 	if = {
			# 		limit = {
			# 			MON = {
			# 				exists = yes
			# 			}
			# 		}
			# 		declare_war_on = {
			# 			target = MON
			# 			type = annex_everything
			# 		}
			# 	}
			# 	if = {
			# 		limit = {
			# 			TAN = {
			# 				exists = yes
			# 			}
			# 		}
			# 		declare_war_on = {
			# 			target = TAN
			# 			type = annex_everything
			# 		}
			# 	}
			# }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = qing_chosen
		set_global_flag = QIN_chosen
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Support Chinese Revolution
		name = ww1_xinhai.2.b
		news_event = { id = kis_news.107 hours = 3 	}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.21
			}
			# QIN = {
			# 	if = {
			# 		limit = {
			# 			MON = {
			# 				exists = yes
			# 			}
			# 		}
			# 		declare_war_on = {
			# 			target = MON
			# 			type = annex_everything
			# 		}
			# 	}
			# 	if = {
			# 		limit = {
			# 			TAN = {
			# 				exists = yes
			# 			}
			# 		}
			# 		declare_war_on = {
			# 			target = TAN
			# 			type = annex_everything
			# 		}
			# 	}
			# }
		}
		set_global_flag = CHI_chosen		
		CHI = {
			change_tag_from = QIN
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = roc_chosen
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
	}
}
#Changsha Uprising
country_event = {
	id = ww1_xinhai.12
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends }
		CHI = {
			exists = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {

		# load_oob = PRC_1911_Wuchang
		
		set_state_owner = 602
		set_state_owner = 893
		set_province_controller = 7101
		set_province_controller = 7097
		set_province_controller = 10517
		
		load_oob = PRC_1911_uprising2_hunan
		load_oob = PRC_1911_uprising2_hunan_minbing
	}
}

#Shanghai Uprising
country_event = {
	id = ww1_xinhai.17
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends }
		CHI = {
			exists = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_state_owner = 613
		set_province_controller = 7014
		set_province_controller = 12076
		load_oob = PRC_1911_uprising2_shanghai
		load_oob = PRC_1911_uprising2_shanghai_minbing
		
		set_global_flag = QIN_third_uprising
		set_global_flag = QIN_first_second_up
		promote_character = CHI_huang_xing
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_revolution
		set_country_flag = second_uprising
		
		QIN = {
			set_country_flag = second_uprising
			CHI_chen_bingkun = {
				set_nationality = CHI
			}
		}
	}
}

#SHIKAI ASKS EMPEROR TO ABDICATE
####################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_xinhai.4
	title = ww1_xinhai.4.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_yuan_cabinet
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		has_war_with = CHI
		has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = xinhai_compromise_fail
			has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_dont_trigger_xinhai_again
		}
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_defection
			# we are about to die
			surrender_progress > 0.7
			CHI = {
				controls_state = 608
			}
			# yuan dont want to waste beiyang troops
			AND = {
				casualties > 100000
				surrender_progress > 0.25
			}
			AND = {
				casualties > 300000
				CHI = { surrender_progress < 0.1 }
			}
			# yuan has another plan :)
			# historical trigger
			AND = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = schemer_yuan
				surrender_progress > 0.10
				NOT = { has_idea = QIN_idea_xinhai_revolution }
				CHI = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_stand_with_tongmenghui
					OR = {
						controls_state = 592
						controls_state = 598
						controls_state = 620
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_sun_yatsen
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#AND = {
			#	has_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_2
			#	fascism > 0.75
			#}
		}
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_yuan_shikai
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_government = neutrality
		has_country_flag = third_uprising
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.4.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_dont_trigger_xinhai_again
		remove_ideas = QIN_idea_xuantong_young
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_xinhai.4.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = ww1_xinhai.10 }
			CHI_yuan_shikai = { # no more loyal(ish) prime minister role
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.4.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		trigger = { has_government = neutrality }
		add_war_support = -0.15
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -200
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.35
		}
		# clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_army_deployed
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
			disband = no
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai
		# custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_cancel_invite_shikai
		CHI_yuan_shikai = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
		
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = QIN_neutrality_cabinet_party
			name = QIN_neutrality_cabinet_party
		}
		remove_ideas = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			target = CHI
			size = 0.4
			target_organization = 1
			source_organization = 1
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = qing_allegiance }
			}
			set_nationality = CHI
		}
	}
}

#THIRD UPRISING
country_event = {
	id = ww1_xinhai.5
	title = ww1_xinhai.5.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_street
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = {
			flag = QIN_third_uprising
			days > 30
		}
		CHI = { exists = yes }
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = QIN_third_uprising
			#QIN = { remove_ideas =  QIN_idea_xinhai_revolution }
			if = {
				limit = {
					CHI = { exists = yes } 
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_state_owner = 598
					set_capital = { state = 598 }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = QIN
							is_controlled_by = CHI
							OR = {
								region = 15
								region = 144
								region = 164
								region = 165
							}
						}
						set_state_owner_to = CHI
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = QIN
							infrastructure < 5
							OR = {
								state = 325
								state = 603
								region = 165
							}
						}
						
						transfer_state_to = CHI
						
					}
					#if = {
					#	limit = {
					#		QIN = { has_completed_focus = QIN_consolidate_the_army }
					#	}
					#	every_state = {
					#		limit = {
					#			is_owned_by = QIN
					#			infrastructure < 5
					#			OR = {
					#				region = 200
					#				region = 145
					#			}
					#		}
					#		
					#		transfer_state_to = CHI
					#		
					#	}
					#}
					QIN = {
						CHI_sun_yatsen = {
							set_nationality = CHI
						}
						set_country_flag = third_uprising
						every_character = {
							limit = {
								has_character_flag = xinhai_revolution_allegiance
							}
							set_nationality = CHI
						}
					}
					CHI = {
						# if = {
						# 	limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_easy_mode } }
							# load_oob = PRC_1911_uprising5
						# }
						CHI_sun_yatsen = {
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
								promote_character = tridemism
						 		add_country_leader_trait = father_of_the_republic
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = tridemism
										traits = { father_of_the_republic }
										desc = CHI_sun_yatsen_desc
									}
								}
							}
						}
						set_country_flag = third_uprising
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.5.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI_sun_yatsen = {
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			add_state_claim = 330
			# if = {

			}

			}
		}
		change_tag_from = FROM
	}

		name = ww1_xinhai.10.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_defection }
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 0

				add = 5

				add = 1000

				}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_popular_support
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = CHI_trait_accepted_monarch
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_trait = unpopular_monarch
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_or_subject_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					region = 15
					region = 165
					state = 602
					state = 890
					state = 893
				}
				is_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = yes
		}
	}
}

							}
						}

								ideology = stratocracy
							}
						}
					}
				}

					}
				}
				if = {

						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = revolutionary_nationalism }

						}

									ideology = revolutionary_nationalism

										revolutionary_general

								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}

							}
						}

					}
				}

							producer = QIN

						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {

				set_province_controller = 9776

			}
		}

# DEATH OF YUAN SHIKAI

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.10
	title = ww1_china.10.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.10.d
		trigger = {
			CHI = { has_country_flag = xinhai_victory }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.10.d2
		trigger = {
			QIN = { has_country_flag = xinhai_victory }
		}
	}
	picture = QIN_report_event_qing_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				QIN = { has_country_flag = xinhai_victory }
			}
			date > 1917.8.1
		}
		else = {
			date > 1916.5.1
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
			set_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
			set_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_focus_tree = china_focus
				}
				# Beiyang Government
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_republican_plot
						}
						remove_ideas = CHI_idea_republican_plot
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_stable_republic
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = CHI_idea_stable_republic
							add_idea = CHI_idea_unstable_republic
						}
					}
					# Empire of China
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_hongxian_empire
							NOT = { has_global_flag = hongxian_failed }
						}
						CHI_beiyang_triumvirate = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									desc = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate_desc
									traits = { CHI_beiyang_triumvirate }
								}
							}
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = stratocracy
									desc = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate_desc
									traits = { CHI_beiyang_triumvirate }
								}
							}
						}
						CHI_duan_qirui = {
							set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
								slot = political_advisor
								value = no
							}
						}
						activate_advisor = CHI_duan_qirui_political
						CHI_feng_guozhang = {
							set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
								slot = political_advisor
								value = no
							}
						}
						activate_advisor = CHI_feng_guozhang_political
						CHI_wang_shizhen = {
							set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
								slot = political_advisor
								value = no
							}
						}
						activate_advisor = CHI_wang_shizhen_political
					}
					# Republic of China
					else = {
						CHI_duan_qirui = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
								promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = authoritarian_democracy
										desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = stratocracy
								}
								promote_character = stratocracy
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = stratocracy
										desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
									}
								}
							}
						}
						CHI_li_yuanhong = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
								promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = authoritarian_democracy
										desc = CHI_li_yuanhong_desc
									}
								}
							}
						}
						unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
					}
				}
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
					}
				}
				country_event =  ww1_china.256
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.10.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = QIN
				has_country_flag = xinhai_victory
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.15
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_kuomintang_state = yes
					has_government = democratic
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.11
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		GZC = {
			exists = no
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	immediate = {
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
			}
			CHI_liu_xianshi = {
				set_nationality = GZC
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = { 
						ideology = warlordism 
						traits = { protector_guizhou }
						}
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = { 
						ideology = stratocracy 
					traits = { protector_guizhou }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GZC = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 603
						}
					}
					add_core_of = GZC
					GZC = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
					}
					CHI_liu_xianshi = {
						set_nationality = GZC
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						CHI = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## Qi Xieyuan
# Warlord Era - JNC (Jiangsu)
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.20
	title = ww1_china.20.t
	desc = ww1_china.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	trigger = {
		tag = ZHC
		has_global_flag = second_zhili_fengtian_war_end
		has_war = no
		NOT = {
			owns_state = 608 #Beijing
			country_exists = JNC
		}
		OR = {
			owns_state = 598
			owns_state = 606
			owns_state = 613
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = luoyang_clique
				}
				set_nationality = JNC
			}
			JNC = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = { has_character = ZHC_qi_xieyuan }
					ZHC_qi_xieyuan = {				
						set_nationality = JNC
						promote_leader = yes
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = warlordism
								traits = { charismatic_warlord }
							}
						}
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
								traits = { charismatic_warlord }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
						OR = {
							state = 598
							state = 606
							state = 613
							state = 1016
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = ROOT
					add_core_of = PREV
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				inherit_technology = ZHC
				set_truce = {
					target = ZHC
					days = 365
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = ZHC_neutrality_party
					name = ZHC_neutrality_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = ZHC_neutrality_party
					name = ZHC_neutrality_party
				}
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_army
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_reorganized_military_industry
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_chinese_unity
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_local_military_development3
				ZHC = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_army_size = {
								size > 20
							}
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = PREV
							size = 0.15
							target_organization = 1
							source_organization = 1
							air_ratio = 0
							navy_ratio = 0
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Jiangxujun"
					division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_army_size = { size < 12 }
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Jiangxujun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.7	start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							count = 7
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.20.a
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.20.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		JNC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.21
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		SDC = {
			exists = no
		}
		JNC = {
			exists = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		has_global_flag = qing_oppress_cliques
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	immediate = {
		SDC = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = { is_china_or_warlord = yes }
					OR = {
						state = 597
						state = 872
					}
				}
				add_core_of = PREV
				transfer_state_to = PREV
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_zhang_huaizhi
				}
				CHI_zhang_huaizhi = {
					set_nationality = SDC
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = warlordism }
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = stratocracy }
					}
				}
			}
			load_oob = CHI_warlord
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					count = 4
				}
			}
			inherit_technology = QIN
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 5000
				producer = QIN
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = tech_support
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = QIN
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

#WARLORD ERA - SHN (SHAANXI)
# Warlord Era - YLN (Yulin/Jing Yuexi)

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.22
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = qing_oppress_cliques
			country_exists = ANC
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 25
	}
	immediate = {
		SHN = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yang_hucheng
				}
				CHI_yang_hucheng = {
					set_nationality = SHN
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_hu_jingyi
				}
				CHI_hu_jingyi = {
					set_nationality = SHN
				}
			}
			add_state_core = 942
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 622
							# state = 942
							state = 890
						}
					}
					add_core_of = SHN
					transfer_state_to = SHN
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 4
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = ANC
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = ANC
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = ANC
							}
						}
						ANC = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
							# puppet shaanxi (Chen Shufan)
							if = {
								limit = { country_exists = SHN }
								SHN = { get_current_government_type = yes }
								set_autonomy = {
									target = SHN
									autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
								}
								SHN = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
							}
						}
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = democratic
							size = 0.2
							states = { 622 }
							keep_all_characters = yes
							PREV = {
								SHN_yu_youren = {
									set_nationality = PREV.PREV
								}
								SHN_yang_hucheng = {
									set_nationality = PREV.PREV
								}
							}
							SHN_yu_youren = {
								promote_character = social_democracy
								promote_character = reformist_socialism
							}
							add_ideas = standing_alone
							set_cosmetic_tag = SHN_pacification
						}
						SHN = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									is_subject = yes
									has_civil_war = yes
								}
								every_enemy_country = {
									limit = {
										original_tag = PREV
									}
									PREV = {
										OVERLORD = {
											add_to_war = {
												targeted_alliance = PREV
												enemy = PREV.PREV
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		YLN = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 622
							state = 942
							state = 890
						}
					}
					add_core_of = YLN
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 942
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = YLN
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = ANC
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = ANC
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = ANC
							}
						}
						ANC = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.24
	title = ww1_china.24.t
	desc = ww1_china.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	trigger = {
		tag = ZHC
		has_global_flag = second_zhili_fengtian_war_end
		has_war = no
		NOT = {
			owns_state = 608 #Beijing
		}
		OR = {
			owns_state = 595
			owns_state = 596
			owns_state = 1062
		}
		country_exists = JNC
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = southern_luoyang_clique
				}
				set_nationality = FJN
			}
			FJN = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
						neutrality = 78
						fascism = 10
						democratic = 12
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = { has_character = ZHC_sun_chuanfang }
					ZHC_sun_chuanfang = {					
						set_nationality = FJN
						promote_leader = yes
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = warlordism
								traits = { smiling_tiger zhili_allegiance }

							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes

							}
						}

							state = 595

							state = 1062
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = ROOT
					add_core_of = PREV
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}

				}

				add_ideas = CHI_idea_reorganized_military_industry

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.25
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		FNG = {
			exists = no
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	immediate = {
		FNG = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						region = 155
						NOT = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
							state = 1045
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FNG
					if = {
						limit = {
							owner = {
								is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = FNG
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							country_exists = QIN
							CHI = { has_idea = QIN_idea_fractured_empire }
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								# state = 328
								state = 610
								state = 717
								state = 908
								state = 910
								# state = 1045
							}
						}
						add_core_of = FNG
						transfer_state_to = FNG
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			load_oob = CHI_warlord
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					count = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = QIN
				}
				inherit_technology = QIN
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = QIN
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = QIN
					}
				}
				QIN = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = FNG
						size = 0.1
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					inherit_technology = CHI
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = CHI
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = CHI
						}
					}
					get_current_government_type = yes
					CHI = {
						set_truce = {
							target = PREV
							days = 330
						}
						set_autonomy = {
							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = FNG
							size = 0.1
							target_organization = 1
							source_organization = 1
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
					restore_previous_government_type = yes
				}
			}
		}
		JLN = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = QIN_meng_enyuan }
				QIN_meng_enyuan = { set_nationality = JLN }
			}
			QIN_meng_enyuan = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = warlordism
						traits = { hairpin_general }
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
						traits = { hairpin_general }
					}
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
							state = 1045
						}
					}
					add_core_of = JLN
					if = {
						limit = {
							owner = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
						}
						transfer_state_to = JLN
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			load_oob = CHI_warlord
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					count = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				}
				inherit_technology = QIN

					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 2500
					producer = QIN
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 250
						producer = QIN
					}
				}
				QIN = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				else = {
					inherit_technology = CHI
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment

country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.27.t
	desc = ww1_china.27.d
	id = ww1_china.27
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_cavalry
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = MON
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 330
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_army_restrictions
					NOT = { owns_state = 608 }
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = russian_civil_war
		SOV = {
			exists = yes
			has_government = communism
		}
		has_global_flag = kolchak_dead
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = RUS_roman_ungern_sternberg
				}
				RUS_roman_ungern_sternberg = {
					set_nationality = MON
					promote_leader = yes
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							traits = {
								spirit_of_genghis
								lunatic
							}
						}
					}
				}			
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = TBK_boris_rezukhin
				}
				TBK_boris_rezukhin = {
					set_nationality = MON
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ALT = {
						exists = no
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = ALT_aleksandr_kaygorodov
					}
					ALT_aleksandr_kaygorodov = {
						set_nationality = MON
					}
				}
			}
			MON = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject = yes }
					OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PREV }
				}
				transfer_state = 330
				transfer_state = 329
				transfer_state = 982
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_ideas = MON_bogd_khan_sternberg
				remove_ideas = MON_divided_rule
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 45
					communism = 5
					democratic = 11
					neutrality = 39
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = MON_neutrality_party
					name = MON_neutrality_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = MON_ungern_party
					name = MON_ungern_party
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = MON_Ungern
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
					}
					remove_state_core = 329
					remove_state_core = 330
					remove_state_claim = 329
					remove_state_claim = 330
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			any_state = {
				OR = {
					state = 563
					state = 564
				}
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = SOV
				}
				is_controlled_by = SOV
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			BYA = {
				has_war_with = SOV
				surrender_progress > 0.10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.27.a
		trigger = {
			tag = MON
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = MON_ungern_party
				name = MON_ungern_party
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			RUS_roman_ungern_sternberg = {
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.27.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = MON }
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_manpower = -1100
		effect_tooltip = {
			MON = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism

					name = MON_ungern_party

 		tag = CHI

 	}
 	fire_only_once = yes

						state = 595

						state = 612
						state = 613
						state = 983

						#Mongol
						state = 330
						state = 329
						state = 982
					}
				}
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {

					is_subject_of = ROOT
					NOT = { tag = ZHC }
				}

					set_autonomy = {

						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				set_truce = {
					target = ROOT
					days = 365
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.28.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_government_divided

					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {

							region = 143

							region = 164
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = ZHC
						}
						to_state = 614
					}
				}
			}
			ANC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = zhili_released }
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = ZHC
						size = 0.5
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1

						army_ratio = 0.5
						navy_ratio = 0.5
						air_ratio = 0.5
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_capital = { state = 608 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = FNG
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							region = 155
						}
						add_core_of = FNG
						transfer_state_to = FNG
						set_demilitarized_zone = no
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = PREV }
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV

					}
				}

						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = ANC
						}
						to_state = 608
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = zhili_released
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_china.41
					hours = 10

# UNITED CHINA - SHARE PROBLEMS WITH WARLORDS

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.35
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		is_chinese_warlord = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = part_of_china }
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = MAN
			}
			NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	immediate = {
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
		set_country_flag = part_of_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				OVERLORD = { has_country_flag = part_of_china }
			}
			copy_warlord_problem = yes
			add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
			add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation5
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation4
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation3
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation2
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_inflation5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption3
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption2
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_army_corruption
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
			add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = MAN_banditry
						has_idea = CHI_idea_merchant_army
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_banditry
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						num_of_factories > 4
						tag = FNG
						tag = GXC
						tag = ANC
						tag = ZHC
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_rampant_opiate_addiction
			}
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_army_hidden
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.38.t
	desc = ww1_china.38.d
	id = ww1_china.38
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_street
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.38.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
					}
					CHI_yuan_shikai = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
							army = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
						}
						set_character_name = CHI_yuan_shikai
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = personalistic_dictatorship
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
						}
						remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					}
				}
			}
			NPA = {
				remove_ideas = standing_alone
				every_character = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_character_flag = dont_transfer
							is_character = CHI_cai_e
							is_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
						}
					}
					clr_character_flag = dont_transfer
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
				if = {
					limit = { original_tag = YUN }
					every_core_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { state = 325 }
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Minbing"
						disband = yes
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Zhejiangjun"
						disband = yes
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Sichuanjun"
						disband = yes
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Shaanxijun"
						disband = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = GDC
							NOT = { country_exists = GXC }
						}
						CHI = {
							annex_country = {
								target = GDC
								transfer_troops = no
							}
						}
					}
					white_peace = CHI
					dismantle_faction = yes
					clr_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
					YUN_luo_peijin = {
						set_nationality = SCC
					}
					SCC = {
						YUN_luo_peijin = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
								promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = stratocracy
								}
								promote_character = stratocracy
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = stratocracy
									}
								}
							}
						}
						get_current_government_type = yes
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								is_demilitarized_zone = no
								NOT = { state = 1066 }
							}
							set_demilitarized_zone = yes
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SCC
						autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
						freedom_level = 0.2
					}
					SCC = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = CHI_fascism_party
				name = CHI_fascism_party
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = NPA
					is_claimed_by = NPA
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = NPA
			remove_claim_by = NPA
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = NPA
			transfer_troops = no
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = warlord_era
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_army_hidden
			country_event = ww1_china.2
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
					}
				}
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
						promote_character = tridemism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = tridemism
								traits = { father_of_the_republic }
								desc = CHI_sun_yatsen_desc
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_unit_leader = yes
						is_field_marshal = no
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_jiang_baili
					}
					CHI_jiang_baili = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
				}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_china.98
				days = 10
			}
			unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 40
				neutrality = 50
				fascism = 8
				communism = 2
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_stability = 0.30
			set_war_support = 0.25
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_kuomintang
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = CHI_kuomintang
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_replace_governors
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_reorganization_loans
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_expand_state_arsenals
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_increase_army_influence
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_presidential_loyalty
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_suppress_nationalists
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_parliament_liquidation
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_maintain_status_quo
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			CHI = {

					targeted_alliance = GXC
					enemy = CHI
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_sun_yatsen_president
			}
		}
	}

		trigger = { is_ai = no }

					has_subject = QZC
				}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.43
	title = ww1_china.43.t
	desc = ww1_china.43.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_duan_and_feng
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ANC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					}
					remove_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					ZHC = { add_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president }
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								OVERLORD = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
							}
						}
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					set_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor
					white_peace = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FNG = { has_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor }
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = FNG
						size = 0.3
						navy_ratio = 0
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								# to event
								# state = 606
								# state = 607
								# state = 891
								state = 609
								state = 610
								state = 611
								state = 612
								state = 983
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = FNG
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = ZHC
						size = 0.75
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = ZHC
						size = 0.6
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_xu_shichang
					}
					CHI_xu_shichang = {
						set_nationality = ZHC
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = ANC_li_houji
					}
					ANC_li_houji = {
						set_nationality = ZHC
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_liang_shiyi
					}
					CHI_liang_shiyi = {
						set_nationality = ZHC
					}
				}
				transfer_navy = {
					target = ZHC
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							state = 329
							state = 330
							state = 595
							state = 596
							state = 613
							state = 622
							state = 982
							state = 983
							state = 1062
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ZHC
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = SHN
					}
					SHN = {
						if = {
							limit = { is_subject = yes }
							OVERLORD = {
								end_puppet = PREV
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_character = SHN_chen_shufan
							}
							SHN_chen_shufan = {
								remove_country_leader_role = {
									ideology = warlordism
								}
								remove_country_leader_role = {
									ideology = stratocracy
								}
								set_nationality = ANC
							}
						}
						get_current_government_type = yes
					}
					ZHC = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = SHN
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
						}
					}
					SHN = {
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
						SHN_liu_zhenhua = {
							promote_character = warlordism
							promote_character = stratocracy
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 143
							region = 144
							region = 164
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = ANC
								is_in_faction_with = ANC
								is_subject_of = ANC
							}
						}
						to_state = 613
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_army_size = { size < 10 }
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Zhejiangjun"
						division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }

							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							field_gun_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
							field_gun_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
							cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
							cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
							cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }

							engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Zhejiangjun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.7	start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							count = 10
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 330
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = { is_core_of = MON }
						transfer_state_to = MON
					}
					MON = {
						get_current_government_type = yes
						set_country_flag = protectorate
					}
					608 = {
						owner = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = MON
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_integrated_protectorate
							}
						}
					}
					MON = {
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
			}
			ZHC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					dismantle_faction = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ANC = { has_character = HNC_zhang_jingyao }

					limit = {
						ANC = { has_character = ANC_wang_haoji }
					}
					ANC_wang_haoji = { set_nationality = ZHC }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ANC = { has_character = ANC_jin_yune }
					}
					ANC_jin_yune = { set_nationality = ZHC }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ANC = { has_character = ANC_tian_zhongyu }
					}
					ANC_tian_zhongyu = { set_nationality = ZHC }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ANC = { has_character = ANC_wang_ruqin }
					}
					ANC_wang_ruqin = { set_nationality = ZHC }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = ww1_china.254
					hours = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						country_exists = XSM
						country_exists = GAN
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
						OR = {
							state = 283
							state = 616
							state = 621
						}
					}
					755 = {
						owner = {
							transfer_state = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PREV
					owner = {
						is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = no
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ZHC
				remove_core_of = PREV
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = PREV
				}
				add_claim_by = ZHC
				remove_claim_by = PREV
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ANC
						has_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = ANC
							has_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor
						}
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_china.44
					days = 3
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = zhili_anhui_war_end
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.43.a
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.43.b

			is_ai = no

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.44
	title = ww1_china.44.t
	desc = ww1_china.44.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_street
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ZHC = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			ZHC = {
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.44.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#FIRST ZHILI-FENGTIAN WAR

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.45
	title = ww1_china.45.t
	desc = ww1_china.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	# trigger = {
	# 	original_tag = ZHC
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_global_flag = second_zhili_fengtian_war
	# 	}
	# 	OR = {
	# 		has_global_flag = first_zhili_fengtian_war
	# 		has_war_with = FNG
	# 	}
	# }
	# fire_only_once = yes
	# mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.45.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { original_tag = ZHC }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ZHC
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ANC
				NOT = { has_war_with = FNG }
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = FNG
				enemy = ZHC
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = first_zhili_fengtian_war }
			}
			set_global_flag = first_zhili_fengtian_war
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FNG
				type = annex_everything
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				FNG = {
					country_event = ww1_china.45
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = ANC
						}
						ANC = { country_event = ww1_china.45 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#END OF FIRST ZHILI-FENGTIAN WAR

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.46
	title = ww1_china.46.t
	desc = ww1_china.46.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_street
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FNG = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = JLN
					}
					JLN = {
						if = {
							limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
							leave_faction = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								OVERLORD = {
									is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
								}
							}
						}
						has_war_with = PREV
						NOT = { tag = JLN }
					}
					white_peace = PREV
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 90
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 15
							region = 143
							region = 144
							region = 152
							region = 164
							region = 165
							region = 200
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ZHC
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.46.a
	}
}

					}

							owner = PREV

							count = 2
						}
					}

							has_idea = CHI_banditry
						}
						remove_ideas = CHI_banditry
					}
					add_ideas = CHI_idea_merchant_army

								num_of_factories > 4

								tag = GXC

								tag = ZHC
							}
							NOT = { has_idea = CHI_rampant_opiate_addiction }
						}

					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_china_or_warlord = yes
							owns_state = 599
						}
						KMT = {
							declare_war_on = {
								target = PREV
								type = independence_wargoal
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { country_exists = QZC }
						KMT = {
							declare_war_on = {
								target = QZC
								type = annex_everything
							}
						}
						GXC = {
							declare_war_on = {
								target = QZC
								type = annex_everything
							}
						}
					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_china_or_warlord = yes
						}
						set_truce = {
							target = PREV
							days = 365
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = KMT }
		}
	}

# DEATH OF SUN YAT-SEN
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.54
	title = ww1_china.54.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.54.d
		trigger = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.54.d_alt
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_sun_yatsen_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
		}
		date > 1925.3.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			set_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
			set_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				}
				CHI_hu_hanmin = {
					set_character_name = CHI_hu_hanmin
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
						promote_character = tridemism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = tridemism
								traits = { conservative_nationalist }
								desc = CHI_hu_hanmin_desc
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				suspend_elections = yes
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead }
				}
				country_event = ww1_china.257
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.54.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag }
				promote_character = CHI_hu_hanmin
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				any_character = {
					is_country_leader = yes
					has_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.54.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag }
				promote_character = CHI_hu_hanmin
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				any_character = {
					is_country_leader = yes
					has_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
						is_in_faction_with = PREV
						is_subject_of = PREV
					}
				}
				send_embargo = PREV
				PREV = {
					create_wargoal = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CSR = { change_tag_from = PREV }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.60
	title = ww1_china.60.t
	desc = ww1_china.60.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GMJ
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
					has_cosmetic_tag = GXC_KMT
				}
			}
			white_peace = GMJ
			set_truce = {
				target = GMJ
				days = 180
			}
			set_country_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war_participants
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = JNC
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
					has_cosmetic_tag = GXC_KMT
				}
			}
			white_peace = JNC
			set_truce = {
				target = JNC
				days = 180
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = FJN
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
					has_cosmetic_tag = GXC_KMT
				}
			}
			white_peace = FJN
			set_truce = {
				target = FJN
				days = 180
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = FNG
					is_owned_by = GMJ
				}
				OR = {
					region = 144
					region = 164
					region = 165
				}
			}
			ZHC = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX = { has_country_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war_participants }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = GMJ
					OR = {
						state = 621
					}
				}
				SHX = {	
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SHN
				}
				SHN = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_subject = yes }
						OVERLORD = {
							end_puppet = PREV
						}
					}
					get_current_government_type = yes
				}
				SHX = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SHN
						autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					}
				}
				SHN = {
					restore_previous_government_type = yes
					SHN_liu_zhenhua = {
						promote_character = warlordism
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = GMJ
					is_owned_by = ZHC
				}
				OR = {
					state = 610
					state = 611
					state = 612
					state = 983
				}
			}
			FNG = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
				OR = {
					state = 283
				}
			}
			GMJ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_owned_by = GMJ }
				is_core_of = GMJ
			}
			remove_core_of = GMJ
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_owned_by = GMJ }
				is_claimed_by = GMJ
			}
			remove_claim_by = GMJ
		}
		set_global_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war_end
		GMJ = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 609
				}
				PREV = {
					transfer_navy = {
						target = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.60.a
	}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.62
	title = ww1_china.62.t
	desc = ww1_china.62.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = MAN_japanese_advisers
			has_idea = CHI_FNG_idea_kwantung_army
			any_neighbor_country = {
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_subject_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		has_character = FNG_zhang_zuolin
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.62.a
		retire_character = FNG_zhang_zuolin
		FNG_zhang_xueliang = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = stratocracy
				}
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
						traits = { young_marshal }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = warlordism
				}
				promote_character = warlordism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = warlordism
						traits = { young_marshal }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = FNG_government
				NOT = { controls_state = 608 }
			}
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
						is_northeast_asian_tag = yes
					}
				}
				news_event = ww1_china.106
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.64
	title = ww1_china.64.t
	desc = ww1_china.64.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_chiang_kai_shek
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war_end }
				}
				set_global_flag = anti_chiang_war_end
				FROM = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = PREV
								is_subject_of = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						white_peace = ROOT
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									state = 615
									state = 621
									state = 622
									state = 890
									state = 942
								}
								OR = {
									region = 143
									region = 144
									region = 164
								}
							}
							add_core_of = ROOT
							transfer_state_to = ROOT
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							dismantle_faction = yes
						}
						ROOT = {
							add_to_faction = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = FNG
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								region = 155
								state = 610
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = FNG
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = GMJ
					}
					GMJ = {
						CHI_yang_hucheng = {
							set_nationality = SHN
						}
						every_subject_country = {
							PREV = { end_puppet = PREV }
						}
					}
					SHN = {
						annex_country = {
							target = GMJ
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
						add_state_core = 622
						add_state_core = 890
						add_state_core = 942
						CHI_yang_hucheng = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = warlordism
								}
								promote_character = warlordism
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = warlordism
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = stratocracy
								}
								promote_character = stratocracy
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = stratocracy
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = conservatism
								}
								promote_character = conservatism
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = conservatism
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.64.a
		add_stability = 0.1
		set_country_flag = reunited_china
		set_global_flag = reunited_china_glov
		set_global_flag = warlord_era_end

	}

		tag = YUN
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_tang_jiyao
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT
		}
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition

				is_kuomintang_state = yes
				has_country_flag = reunited_china
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.67.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
				}
				retire_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
			}
			YUN_long_yun = {
				promote_character = conservatism
				promote_character = stratocracy
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				set_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_kuomintang_state = yes
						AND = {
							is_subject = yes
							OVERLORD = {
								is_kuomintang_state = yes
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							any_allied_country = {
								is_kuomintang_state = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 603 }
				599 = {
					owner = {
						transfer_state = 603
					}
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				}
				ROOT = { get_current_government_type = yes }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
				}
				ROOT = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			YUN_long_yun = {
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.68
	title = ww1_china.68.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.68.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = CHI
				country_exists = ZHC
				country_exists = ANC
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.68.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = CHI
				country_exists = ZHC
				country_exists = ANC
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.68.d3
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		date > 1919.4.1
		has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 12 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
						has_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
				set_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.68.a
		retire_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
		add_political_power = -40
		
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = ZHC_liu_xun
				}
				ZHC_liu_xun = { set_nationality = ANC }
			}
		}

		# Feng Guozhang was president
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			set_country_flag = duan_qirui_president
			set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
			new_term_elections = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				# prepare government divide
				ANC = {
					new_term_elections = yes
					# Duan is president, no need to add ideas
				}
				CHI = {
					new_term_elections = yes
				}
				ZHC = {
					new_term_elections = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war_end }
				}
				set_global_flag = anti_chiang_war_end
				SHX = {
					every_enemy_country = {
						limit = {
							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
						}
						white_peace = PREV
					}
					KMT = {
						every_core_state = {
							add_core_of = PREV.PREV
						}

							limit = {
								is_claimed_by = PREV.PREV
							}
							add_claim_by = PREV.PREV
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = PREV
							size = 0.3
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
						transfer_navy = {
							target = PREV
						}
						every_allied_country = {
							limit = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
							leave_faction = yes
							PREV.PREV = { add_to_faction = PREV }
						}
						every_subject_country = {
							PREV = { end_puppet = PREV }
							if = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										original_tag = MON
										original_tag = TIB
									}
								}
								get_current_government_type = yes
								PREV = {
									set_autonomy = {
										target = PREV
										autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_integrated_protectorate
									}
								}
								restore_previous_government_type = yes
							}
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = KMT
						transfer_troops = no
					}
					set_capital = {
						state = 608
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_BEIPING
					set_country_flag = reunited_china
					set_global_flag = reunited_china_glov
					set_global_flag = warlord_era_end
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = yes
							KMT = { is_ai = no }
						}
						change_tag_from = KMT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.69.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_tt
	}
}

country_event = {

	}

							}
						}
					}

							}
						}
					}
				}

					limit = {

							transfer_state_to = GMJ

							owner = {
								PREV = {
									set_state_owner_to = GMJ
									if = {
										limit = {
											PREV = { has_war_with = ROOT }
										}
										add_contested_owner = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 600
							state = 1046
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = PREV
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
						}
						transfer_state_to = ROOT
					}
					else = {

								}
							}

					}
				}

			CHI_wang_jingwei = {
				if = {

							desc = CHI_wang_jingwei_desc
