country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.72
	title = ww1_china.72.t
	desc = ww1_china.72.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_tongmenghui
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.72.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement
				add_idea = CHI_idea_nationalist_revolution
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = reunited_china
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 598
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = { state = 598 } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_NANJING
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 620
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = { state = 620 } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_WUHAN
			}
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_GUANGZHOU
			}
		}
		CHI_wang_jingwei = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
				promote_character = tridemism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = tridemism
						desc = CHI_wang_jingwei_desc
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = chinese_united_front
				has_country_flag = chinese_united_front
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = tridemism_is_socialism
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_kmt_power_struggle
		new_term_elections = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_chiang_kaishek = {
				promote_leader = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = civilian_dictatorship }
					promote_character = civilian_dictatorship
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = civilian_dictatorship
							traits = { generallissimo }
							desc = CHI_chiang_kaishek_desc
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_revolutionary_army_long
				name = CHI_revolutionary_army
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = liao_zhongkai_dead }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_china.99
					days = 45
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_china.73
				days = 240
			}
		}
	}
}

							target = PREV
							size = 0.2
							target_organization = 1
							source_organization = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				democratic > 0.40
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				fascism < 0.05
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

# DEATH OF CAI E
###########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.82
	title = ww1_china.82.t
	desc = ww1_china.82.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		has_character = CHI_cai_e
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = cai_e_dead
		}
		date > 1916.11.1
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 8 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = CHI_cai_e
			set_country_flag = cai_e_dead
			set_global_flag = cai_e_dead
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
						original_tag = YUN
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character = CHI_tang_jiyao }
					CHI_tang_jiyao = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
							promote_character = stratocracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = stratocracy
									traits = { pillar_south }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = { pillar_south }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character = CHI_liang_qichao }
					CHI_liang_qichao = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
							promote_character = reformist_socialism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = reformist_socialism
									traits = { gentle_scholar }
									desc = CHI_liang_qichao_desc
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
							promote_character = conservatism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = conservatism
									traits = { gentle_scholar }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
						NOT = { has_country_flag = cai_e_dead }
					}
					country_event = ww1_china.258
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.82.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_cai_e
		}
	}
}

# CHINISE UNITED FRONT IN WARLORD ERA
########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.83
	title = ww1_china.83.t
	desc = ww1_china.83.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_qing_forbidden_city
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = QIN
			tag = CHI
			AND = {
				OR = {
					tag = ANC
					tag = ZHC
					tag = FNG
				}
				owns_state = 608
			}
			has_country_flag = reunited_china
		}
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = warlord_era_end
			has_global_flag = chinese_salvation_army
		}
		OR = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			is_in_faction = no
		}
		OR = {
			any_other_country = {
				is_china_or_warlord = no
				is_major = yes
				NOT = { tag = SIK }
				NOT = { tag = MON }
				NOT = { tag = TIB }
				has_offensive_war_with = PREV
			}
			AND = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_subject = no
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PREV = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
						has_government = communism
						else = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
					}
					any_other_country = {
						is_china_or_warlord = no
						is_major = yes
						has_offensive_war_with = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.83.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		# FLAGS
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_salvation_army
			set_country_flag = chinese_salvation_army_leader
		}
		# CREATE FACTION
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			create_faction = chinese_salvation_army
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = chinese_salvation_army_reserve
				}
				set_faction_name = chinese_salvation_army
			}
		}
		# BRING SUBJECT CLIQUES
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = no
					is_major = yes
					has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
				}
				PREV = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = ROOT
						enemy = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# INVITE OTHER CHINESE COUNTRIES
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = PREV
					is_in_faction_with = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					has_government = communism
					else = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_china.84
		}
		# GOOD EFFECTS
		add_war_support = 0.3
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.83.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.89
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					tag = QIN
				}
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = no
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = warlord_era
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = reunited_china
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			has_war_with = FRA
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GER
			# GER = {
			# 	has_completed_focus = GER_chinese_intervention
			# }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = PREV
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					has_war_with = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_to_faction = PREV
		}
	}
}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0

			}
		}
	}

		}

			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
		}
		FROM = {
			add_political_power = 30
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_influence_faction
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PREV
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
			add_to_faction = PREV
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				any_character = {
					is_country_leader = yes
					has_character_flag = federalist_allegiance
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_zhao_hengti
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SIK_sheng_shicai
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_tang_jiyao
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = ZHC_wu_peifu
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					original_tag = SCC
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # NOT GONNA ALLOW YOU
		name = ww1_china.94.b
		add_political_power = 70
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM

		}
		FROM = {
			add_political_power = -30
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_diplomats_malus
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_government = communism
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10

					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}

# Presidential Problem
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.113
	title = ww1_china.113.t
	desc = ww1_china.113.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Side with Duan Qirui
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.113.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = CHI_duan_qirui
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FNG
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord = yes }
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
							state = 1045
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FNG
					transfer_state_to = FNG
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SIK
					country_exists = KUM
				}
				SIK = {
					set_autonomy = {

	}

# Call Guangxi for National Protection
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.114
	title = ww1_china.114.t
	desc = ww1_china.114.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_war_with = CHI
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.114.a
		CHI = {
			CHI_lu_rongting = {
				set_nationality = GXC
			}
			CHI_cen_chunxuan = {
				set_nationality = GXC
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			release = GXC
			add_to_faction = GXC
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						region = 165
					}
					add_core_of = PREV
				}
				CHI_cen_chunxuan = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { butcher_of_officials }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = conservatism
						}
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { butcher_of_officials }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_lu_rongting = {
					promote_leader = yes
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = warlordism
						}
						promote_character = warlordism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = warlordism
								traits = { righteous_theif }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
								traits = { righteous_theif }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Guangxijun"
					division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Guangxijun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.2	start_equipment_factor = 0.6"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 6
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = CHI
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = CHI
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = CHI
					}
				}
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = NPA
					enemy = CHI
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_national_protection
			}
			add_to_faction = GXC
		}
	}
}

				hours = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

# Back to Republic?
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.121
	title = ww1_china.121.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.121.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				CHI_yuan_keding = {
					skill > 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.121.d2
		trigger = {
			CHI_yuan_keding = {
				skill > 1
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_character = CHI_yuan_keding
		has_completed_focus = CHI_second_empire
		has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = NPA
			country_exists = NPA
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.121.a
		retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
		set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
		retire_character = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = yes
			election_frequency = 60
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
						desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_li_yuanhong = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						desc = CHI_li_yuanhong_desc
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
			can_join_factions = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_feng_guozhang = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_wang_shizhen = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
			set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
			set_global_flag = warlord_era
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_army_hidden
			country_event = ww1_china.2
			#set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
					}
				}
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					promote_character = tridemism
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 40
				neutrality = 50
				fascism = 8
				communism = 2
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_china.98
			days = 10
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.121.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = QIN
					exists = yes
				}
				any_country = {

					exists = yes
				}

					exists = yes
				}

					has_cosmetic_tag = QIN
					exists = yes
				}
			}
		}

			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				GER = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

# Cai E Restores Democracy 
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.122
	title = ww1_china.122.t
	desc = ww1_china.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	trigger = {
		# tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_government = fascism
			has_global_flag = hongxian_failed
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.122.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = CHI_cai_e
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = standing_alone
		set_cosmetic_tag = NPA_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
				name = QIN_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_liang_qichao = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
					promote_character = reformist_socialism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = reformist_socialism
							traits = { gentle_scholar }
							desc = CHI_liang_qichao_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_liang_qichao = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
				promote_character = conservatism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
						traits = { gentle_scholar }
						desc = CHI_liang_qichao_desc
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
					name = QIN_progressive_party
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		set_country_flag = national_protection_government
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.122.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = CHI_cai_e
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NPA_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
				name = QIN_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_liang_qichao = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
					promote_character = reformist_socialism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = reformist_socialism
							traits = { gentle_scholar }
							desc = CHI_liang_qichao_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_liang_qichao = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
				promote_character = conservatism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
						traits = { gentle_scholar }
						desc = CHI_liang_qichao_desc
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
					name = QIN_progressive_party
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		set_country_flag = national_protection_government
	}
}

			NOT = {
				original_tag = ENG
				is_subject_of = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.124.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = ENG
				is_subject_of = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.124.a
		FROM = { transfer_state = 746 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {

				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.124.b
		FROM = { country_event = ww1_china.125 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5

					target = FROM

				}
			}

				add = -5

				}
			}
		}
	}

# Northeast Flag Replacement
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.128
	title = ww1_china.128.t
	desc = ww1_china.128.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = KMT
			has_country_leader = {
				character = FNG_zhang_zuolin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.128.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT #JAPAN
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = ww1_china.156
					hours = 3
				}
			}
		}
		KMT = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			every_enemy_country = {
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV.PREV
						enemy = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_core = yes
				NOT = {
					region = 200
					state = 610
					state = 611
					state = 612
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		chinese_flag_replacement = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.128.b
		add_political_power = -75
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_ideas = CHI_FNG_idea_regionalist_sentiment
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_core = yes
				NOT = {
					region = 200
					state = 610
					state = 611
					state = 612
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	}

		}
	}

country_event = {

	desc = ww1_china.134.d

			target = FROM
			modifier = CHI_appeased_us
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_china.135 hours = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				original_tag = JAP
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = FNG
						original_tag = SHX
						original_tag = ZHC
						original_tag = ANC
					}
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
				}	
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_government = communism
				FROM = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					has_government = communism
				}	
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				has_subject = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				FROM = { is_major = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				FROM = { has_country_flag = reunited_china }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.134.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_china.136 hours = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_wargoal_against = FROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Yunnan - Gu Pinzhen get killed
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.138
	title = ww1_china.138.t
	desc = ww1_china.138.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = YUN
		has_country_leader = {
			character = YUN_gu_pinzhen
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.138.a
		retire_character = YUN_gu_pinzhen
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = YUN_luo_peijin
			}
			retire_character = YUN_luo_peijin
		}
		CHI_tang_jiyao = {
			promote_character = stratocracy
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = SCC }
			end_puppet = SCC
			SCC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_demilitarized_zone = yes
						NOT = { state = 1055 }
					}
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = YUN_luo_peijin
					}
					retire_character = YUN_luo_peijin
				}
				SCC_liu_cunhou = {
					promote_character = warlordism
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = SCC
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				white_peace = SCC
			}
			transfer_state = 1066
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.145
	title = ww1_china.145.t
	desc = ww1_china.145.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SWI_assembly_hall
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_government = neutrality
		has_civil_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			has_global_flag = constitutional_protection_war
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.145.a
		add_stability = 0.10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				neutrality > 30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				neutrality > 60
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				neutrality > 80
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.145.b
		add_stability = 0.10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		# Li Yuanhong clique transfered to democratic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_beiyang_government }
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_government
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_beiyang_government2 }
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_government2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_progressive_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
						desc = CHI_li_yuanhong_desc
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				democratic > 10
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				democratic > 30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				democratic > 60
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				democratic > 80
			}
		}
	}
}

# Assassination of Chen Qimei
##############################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.152
	title = ww1_china.152.t
	desc = ww1_china.152.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		has_character = CHI_chen_qimei
		has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		OR = {
			#historical
			AND = {
				has_completed_focus = CHI_second_empire
				has_global_flag = national_protection_war
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
				}
			}
			#ahistorical
			AND = {
				has_government = democratic
				OR = {
					fascism > 0.10
					neutrality > 0.10
				}
				has_civil_war = no
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = national_protection_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_war = no
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.152.a
		retire_character = CHI_chen_qimei
	}
}

# Li Yuanhong Presidency ended
## This is needed when if the Great War is over before Duan's demand to join the war
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.153
	title = ww1_china.153.t
	desc = ww1_china.153.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.153.a
		hidden_effect = {
			ANC = {
				new_term_elections = yes
				# Duan is president, no need to add ideas
			}
			ZHC = {
				new_term_elections = yes
			}
			FNG = {
				new_term_elections = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
					add_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		new_term_elections = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.154
	title = ww1_china.154.t
	desc = ww1_china.154.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_infiltration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 31
					neutrality = 63
					fascism = 4
					communism = 2
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
					name = CHI_national_protection_army
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
					name = CHI_national_protection_army
				}
				NPA = {
					transfer_navy = {
						target = CHI
					}
					every_character = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Minbing"
						disband = yes
					}
					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Zhejiangjun"
						is_locked = no
					}
					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Sichuanjun"
						is_locked = no
					}
					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Shaanxijun"
						is_locked = no
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
						OR = {
							tag = NPA
							is_in_faction_with = NPA
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
						}
						CHI_liu_xianshi = {
							remove_country_leader_role = {
								ideology = warlordism
							}
							remove_country_leader_role = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
							set_nationality = PREV
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character = CHI_lu_rongting
						}
						CHI_lu_rongting = {
							remove_country_leader_role = {
								ideology = warlordism
							}
							remove_country_leader_role = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
							set_nationality = PREV
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character = CHI_chen_jiongming
						}
						CHI_chen_jiongming = {
							set_nationality = PREV
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = PREV
								is_claimed_by = PREV
							}
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					PREV = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
					}
				}
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = beiyang_allegiance
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}	
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = cai_e_dead }
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = revolutionary_nationalism }
							promote_character = revolutionary_nationalism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = revolutionary_nationalism
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
									desc = CHI_cai_e_desc
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { is_field_marshal = no }
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_liang_qichao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { gentle_scholar  }
								desc = CHI_liang_qichao_desc
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead }
					}
					CHI_sun_yatsen = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
							promote_character = tridemism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { father_of_the_republic }
									desc = CHI_sun_yatsen_desc
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
							promote_character = reformist_socialism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = reformist_socialism
									traits = { father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				YUN = { clr_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag }
				set_cosmetic_tag = NPA
				set_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.154.a
		remove_ideas = standing_alone
		add_stability = 0.10
	}
}

							}
						}

						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}

						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}
				}

							is_core_of = PREV
							is_claimed_by = PREV
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = PREV

				retire_character = CHI_cai_e

					target = CHI

					set_nationality = CHI

					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			owns_state = 608
		}
		name = ww1_china.157.a
		set_country_flag = national_pacification_army
		set_global_flag = national_pacification_army
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			set_faction_name = national_pacification_army
			else = {
				create_faction = national_pacification_army
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
			add_country_leader_trait = generallissimo
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_kuomintang_state = no
			NOT = { owns_state = 608 }
		}
		name = ww1_china.157.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			608 = {
				owner = {
					create_faction = national_pacification_army

						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
						}
						remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}

			modifier = {
				add = -100

				}

			modifier = {
				add = -25

					target = FROM
					value > 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_government = communism
				FROM = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM

				}
			}
		}
	}

					}

		add_timed_idea = {

			annex_country = {
				target = TIB
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_1
				amount = -2500
				producer = CHI
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					set_rule = {
						can_join_factions = yes
					}
				}
				FRA = {
					add_to_faction = CHI
				}
			}
			else = {
				CHI = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ENG
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ENG
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
				ENG = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
						country = CHI
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = CHI
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.170.b
		CHI = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_china.171
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

# Tan Yankai Overthrown
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.181
	title = ww1_china.181.t
	desc = ww1_china.181.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HNC
		is_subject = no
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		has_global_flag = CHI_government_split_mission
		has_country_leader = {
			character = HNC_tan_yankai
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.181.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_leader_ideology = tridemism
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = social_liberalism
					}
					promote_character = social_liberalism
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
					}
					clr_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
				}
			}
			HNC_tan_yankai = {
				clr_character_flag = federalist_allegiance
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = conservatism
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = CHI_zhigong_party_long
				name = CHI_zhigong_party
			}
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_character = HNC_tan_yankai
						is_character = HNC_cheng_qian
					}
				}
				set_nationality = GDC
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
	}
}

# Hunan Tang Shengzi
#################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.185
	title = ww1_china.185.t
	desc = ww1_china.185.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.185.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = HNC_tang_shengzhi
				}
				HNC_tang_shengzhi = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
			clear_all_relations = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		HNC_tang_shengzhi = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = conservatism
				}
				promote_character = conservatism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = stratocracy
				}
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				OVERLORD = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_kuomintang_state = no
					owns_state = 620
				}
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				end_puppet = PREV
				PREV = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = neutrality
						keep_all_characters = yes
						size = 0.5
						PREV = {
							every_character = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_character_flag = kmt_allegiance }
								}
								set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 20
							neutrality = 70
							fascism = 10
						}
						CHI_zhao_hengti = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
								promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
								else = {
									add_country_leader_role = {
										promote_leader = yes
										country_leader = {
											ideology = authoritarian_democracy
											
										}
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = social_liberalism
								}
								promote_character = social_liberalism
								else = {
									add_country_leader_role = {
										promote_leader = yes
										country_leader = {
											ideology = social_liberalism
											
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						get_current_government_type = yes
						PREV.PREV = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = PREV
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
								end_civil_wars = no
								end_wars = no
							}
						}
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_zhao_hengti
				}
				CHI_zhao_hengti = {
					remove_advisor_role = {
						slot = army_chief
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				}
			}
		}
		KMT = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			effect_tooltip = {
				puppet = ROOT
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = KMT
							enemy = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 35
						neutrality = 50
						communism = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = warlordism
								traits = { dogmeat_general fengtian_allegiance }
							}
						}
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
								traits = { dogmeat_general fengtian_allegiance }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = FNG_date_junnosuke
					}
					FNG_date_junnosuke = { set_nationality = SDC }
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = FNG_liu_zhennian
					}
					FNG_liu_zhennian = { set_nationality = SDC }
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = FNG_konstantin_nechayev
					}
					FNG_konstantin_nechayev = { set_nationality = SDC }
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = FNG_li_jinglin
					}
					FNG_li_jinglin = { set_nationality = SDC }
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = FNG_xu_yuanquan
					}
					FNG_xu_yuanquan = { set_nationality = SDC }
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = SHN_sun_dianying
					}
					SHN_sun_dianying = { set_nationality = SDC }
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_zhang_huaizhi
					}
					retire_character = CHI_zhang_huaizhi
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 10
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = ROOT
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = yes
							has_army_size = { size > 20 }
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = SDC
							size = 0.2
							target_organization = 1
							source_organization = 1
							air_ratio = 0
							navy_ratio = 0
							stockpile_ratio = 0
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SDC
						autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					}
					copy_government_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.197.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			release_puppet = SDC
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.197.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		effect_tooltip = {
			release_puppet = SDC
		}
		SDC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Guangxi Overthrown
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.211
	title = ww1_china.211.t
	desc = ww1_china.211.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GXC
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		is_kuomintang_state = no
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_lu_rongting
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		any_neighbor_country = {
			is_kuomintang_state = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = second_constitutional_protection_movement
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.211.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = neutrality 
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = GXC_KMT
		GXC_li_zongren = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_kuomintang_state = yes
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						OVERLORD = {
							is_kuomintang_state = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = democratic 
				long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
				name = CHI_kuomintang_party
			}
			GXC_li_zongren = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = conservatism
					}
					promote_character = conservatism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = conservatism
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		KMT = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ROOT
				autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 30
				neutrality = 60
				fascism = 0
				communism = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.211.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		retire_character = GXC_li_zongren
		retire_character = GXC_bai_chongxi
	}

# NPA denounces the Truce
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.215
	title = ww1_china.215.t
	desc = ww1_china.215.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.215.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
					}
					CHI_yuan_shikai = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
							army = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
						}
						set_character_name = CHI_yuan_shikai
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = personalistic_dictatorship
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
						}
						remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					}
				}
			}
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = CHI_fascism_party
				name = CHI_fascism_party
			}
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_unit_leader = yes
						is_field_marshal = no
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							desc = CHI_duan_qirui_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							desc = CHI_li_yuanhong_desc
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_unstable_republic
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 40
			neutrality = 50
			fascism = 8
			communism = 2
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_china.98
			days = 10
		}
		set_stability = 0.30
		set_war_support = 0.25
		unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

			}

				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes

							ideology = reformist_socialism
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			CHI_hu_hanmin = {

# End of Northern Expedition
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.223
	title = ww1_china.223.t
	desc = ww1_china.223.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	trigger = {
		has_capitulated = no
		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = wuhan_government
			has_country_flag = nanjing_government
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			country_exists = ANC
			country_exists = ZHC
			any_enemy_country = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_left_kuomintang_flag
			}
		}
		598 = {
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
		608 = {
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
		620 = {
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
					transfer_navy = {
						target = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								region = 143
								region = 144
								region = 164
								region = 165
								state = 983
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_subject = no
							NOT = {
								tag = FNG
								tag = MAN
								tag = MEN
							}
						}
						get_current_government_type = yes
						ROOT = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = PREV
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
							}
						}
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
						chinese_flag_replacement = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					dismantle_faction = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						exists = yes
					}
					white_peace = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_subject = MON
					}
					MON = {
						get_current_government_type = yes
						ROOT = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = PREV
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
							}
						}
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = FNG
					}
					FNG = {
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_china.62
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_chinese_core = yes
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = GMJ

					limit = {

							state = 597

							state = 872
							state = 890
							state = 891
							region = 200
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = GMJ
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = SHX
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 983
							region = 143
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 597
							state = 745
							state = 746
							state = 872
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = GXC
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 165
							state = 602
							state = 620
							state = 893
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = GXC
				}
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = GZC
				autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
			}
			GZC = {
				add_state_core = 603
				transfer_state = 603
				GZC_zhou_xicheng = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = warlordism
						}
						promote_character = warlordism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = warlordism
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = conservatism
						}
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 70
					democratic = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						region = 165
						NOT = { state = 599 }
					}
				}

							limit = {
								region = 165
								NOT = { state = 599 }
							}
							add_core_of = PREV.PREV
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
						every_character = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_character = GDC_chen_jitang
									is_character = CHI_li_jishen
									is_character = CHI_chen_mingshu

							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = PREV
							size = 0.2
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
					GDC_chen_jitang = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_character = stratocracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = stratocracy
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = conservatism
							}
							promote_character = conservatism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = conservatism
								}
							}
						}
					}
					CHI_li_jishen = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_character = stratocracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes

							}
						}

						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = conservatism
								}

					get_current_government_type = yes
					ROOT = {

							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
						}
					}
					restore_previous_government_type = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 598
				}

					state = 598
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_NANJING
			}
			else = {
				set_capital = {
					state = 620
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_WUHAN
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes

								has_government = fascism
								has_government = communism
								tag = MAN
								tag = MEN
								tag = FNG
								tag = SIK
							}
						}
						any_character = {
							is_country_leader = yes
							has_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_character = {
							is_country_leader = yes
							has_character_flag = kmt_allegiance
						}
					}
					ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
				ROOT = {

				}

				id = ww1_china.61
				hours = 3
			}

					}
					remove_core_of = SCC
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
					add_core_of = XKC
					transfer_state_to = XKC
				}
				SCC_liu_wenhui = { set_nationality = XKC }
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = XKC
					size = 0.20
					target_organization = 1
							source_organization = 1
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						always = yes
					}
				}
				XKC = {
					SCC_liu_wenhui = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = warlordism
							}
							promote_character = warlordism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = warlordism
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_character = stratocracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = stratocracy
								}
							}
						}
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = ROOT
						days = 365
					}
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				release = XKC
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.50
			states = { 605 }
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
			keep_political_party_members = yes
			PREV = {
				SCC_yang_sen = {
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				}
			}
			SCC_yang_sen = {
				promote_character = stratocracy
				promote_character = warlordism
			}
		}
	}
}

		tag = SCC
		has_country_leader = {
			character = YUN_luo_peijin
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = cai_e_dead
		is_subject = yes
		owns_state = 1066
		any_owned_state = {
			NOT = { state = 1066 }
		}
		has_character = SCC_liu_cunhou
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.233.a
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		SCC_liu_cunhou = {
			promote_character = warlordism
			promote_character = stratocracy
		}
		YUN_luo_peijin = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = stratocracy
			}
			set_nationality = YUN
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = YUN
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				transfer_state = 1066
				end_puppet = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
					ROOT = { leave_faction = yes }
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = { is_china_or_warlord = yes }
					white_peace = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# CCP Notice
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.255
	title = ww1_china.255.t
	desc = ww1_china.255.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_protest
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_country_flag = chinese_communist_party
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = chinese_communisty_party
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.255.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					is_china_or_warlord = no
					has_capitulated = no
					is_subject = no
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = syndicalism
						has_country_leader_ideology = anarcho_syndicalism
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = CHI_syndicalist_party_long
				name = CHI_syndicalist_party
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = CHI_communist_party_long
				name = CHI_communist_party
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = CHI_idea_communist_movement
			days = 180
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = CHI_li_dazhao
			}
			CHI_li_dazhao = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = vanguardism }
					promote_character = vanguardism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = vanguardism
							desc = CHI_li_dazhao_desc
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

		}

					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
	}
}

	desc = ww1_china.285.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		any_state = {
			region = 165
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_left_kuomintang_flag
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.285.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 165
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_left_kuomintang_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = OWNER
				}
				transfer_state_to = KMT
			}
			else = {
				set_state_owner_to = KMT
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_left_kuomintang_flag
			}
			add_stability = -0.10
			add_political_power = -200
			transfer_units_fraction = {
				target = ROOT
				size = 0.1
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					always = yes
				}
			}
			transfer_navy = {
				target = ROOT
			}
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_character = CHI_li_jishen
					}
				}
				CHI_li_jishen = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_political_power = 40
	}
}

# The Soviet Ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.294
	title = ww1_china.294.t
	desc = ww1_china.294.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.294.a
		FROM = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = take_state
				generator = { 908 909 910 1005 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_china.295
				hours = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.294.b
		add_political_power = -70
		add_stability = -0.05
		FROM = { add_political_power = 75 }
		CER = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					OR = {
						state = 908
						state = 909
						state = 910
						state = 1005
					}
				}
				add_core_of = PREV
				transfer_state_to = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = sino_soviet_treaty
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = CER
				autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
			}
			CER = {
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_government = communism }
						}
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 40
							neutrality = 60
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = neutrality
							elections_allowed = no
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CER_soviet
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						long_name = CER_chinese_party_long
						name = CER_chinese_party
					}
					every_possible_country = {
						limit = {
							has_character = CHI_zhu_qinglan
						}
						CHI_zhu_qinglan = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
					CHI_zhu_qinglan = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = conservatism
							}
							promote_character = conservatism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = conservatism
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_character = stratocracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = stratocracy
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CER_soviet_agreement
				give_military_access = ROOT
				give_market_access = ROOT
				give_military_access = FROM
				give_market_access = FROM
				break_embargo = FROM
				FROM = { give_guarantee = PREV }
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CER
					autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_concession
				}
			}
			CER = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				give_military_access = ROOT
			}
			give_guarantee = CER
			give_market_access = CER
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_street
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.296.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = khabarovsk_protocol }
			}
			event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_chi = {
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus
							is_subject_of = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus
							is_in_faction_with = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus
						}
					}
					white_peace = PREV
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -200
				add_stability = -0.15
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = PREV
						OR = {
							state = 908
							state = 909
							state = 910
							state = 1005
						}
					}
					remove_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus = {
				add_political_power = 100
				add_stability = 0.05
				CER = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							OR = {
								state = 908
								state = 909
								state = 910
								state = 1005
							}
						}
						add_core_of = PREV
						transfer_state_to = PREV
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = sino_soviet_treaty
					}
					CER = {
						event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_chi = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = PREV
								autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
							}
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_government = communism }
								}
								set_popularities = {
									communism = 40
									neutrality = 60
								}
								set_politics = {
									ruling_party = neutrality
									elections_allowed = no
								}
							}
							set_cosmetic_tag = CER_soviet
							set_party_name = {
								ideology = neutrality
								long_name = CER_chinese_party_long
								name = CER_chinese_party
							}
							every_possible_country = {
								limit = {
									has_character = CHI_zhu_qinglan
								}
								CHI_zhu_qinglan = {
									set_nationality = PREV.PREV
								}
							}
							CHI_zhu_qinglan = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									}
									promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
								}
								else = {
									add_country_leader_role = {
										promote_leader = yes
										country_leader = {
											ideology = authoritarian_democracy
										}
									}
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										has_ideology = conservatism
									}
									promote_character = conservatism
								}
								else = {
									add_country_leader_role = {
										promote_leader = yes
										country_leader = {
											ideology = conservatism
										}
									}
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										has_ideology = stratocracy
									}
									promote_character = stratocracy
								}
								else = {
									add_country_leader_role = {
										promote_leader = yes
										country_leader = {
											ideology = stratocracy
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						add_ideas = CER_soviet_agreement
						give_military_access = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_chi
						give_market_access = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_chi
						give_military_access = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus
						give_market_access = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus
						break_embargo = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus
						event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus = { give_guarantee = PREV }
					}
				}
				else = {
					event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_rus = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = CER
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_concession
						}
					}
					CER = {
						drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
						give_military_access = event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_chi
					}
					event_target:fengtian_soviet_war_chi = {
						give_guarantee = CER
						give_market_access = CER
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = khabarovsk_protocol
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.298
	title = ww1_china.298.t

		has_global_flag = karakhan_manifesto

					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
				}
				is_subject = yes
				has_cosmetic_tag = CER_high_commission

			}
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OVERLORD = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
				}
			}
		}
		563 = {
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}

			owner = {
				is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			}
		}
		716 = {
			owner = {
				is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = chinese_eastern_railway_incident
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			}
		}

	}

				}
			}

				if = {

						ruling_party = neutrality

					name = CER_chinese_party
				}
				every_possible_country = {

					}

						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
				CHI_zhu_qinglan = {

					else = {

							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = conservatism
						}
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {

						}

					else = {

					}

			}

# Long March
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.300
	title = ww1_china.300.t
	desc = ww1_china.300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_mountain
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = chinese_soviet_republic
		has_global_flag = long_march
		is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
		owns_state = 622
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			country_exists = PRC
			any_other_country = {
				is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC = {
				transfer_state = 622
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
					}
					white_peace = ROOT
					set_truce = {
						target = ROOT
						days = 365
					}
				}
				remove_ideas = standing_alone
				load_oob = CSR_1931
				PRC_mao_zedong = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = agrarian_socialism
						}
						promote_character = agrarian_socialism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = agrarian_socialism
								traits = { cornered_fox }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = long_march
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.300.a
		send_embargo = PRC
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.300.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		send_embargo = PRC
		PRC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}
