country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.311
	title = ww1_china.311.t
	desc = ww1_china.311.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		610 = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_subject_of = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_mountain
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.311.a
		trigger = {
			is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 610
			}
			617 = {
				owner = {
					add_state_core = 610
					transfer_state = 610
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.311.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Tanggu Truce
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.312
	title = ww1_china.312.t
	desc = ww1_china.312.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_japanese_handshake
	trigger = {
		609 = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_subject_of = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.312.a
		trigger = {
			is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 609
			}
			609 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
		}
		set_truce = {
			target = FROM
			days = 365
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.312.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
		608 = {
			owner = {
				ROOT = {
					set_truce = {
						target = FROM
						days = 365
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inner Mongolian Independence
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.313
	title = ww1_china.313.t
	desc = ww1_china.313.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		611 = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_subject_of = FROM
					tag = MEN
				}
			}
		}
		612 = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_subject_of = FROM
					tag = MEN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_cavalry
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = MEN }
				}
				611 = { transfer_state_to = FROM }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = MON
								is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
								original_tag = FROM
								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}
						OR = {
							state = 612
							state = 983
						}
					}
					MEN = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
						every_state = {
							limit = { is_core_of = MON }
							add_claim_by = PREV
						}
						add_ideas = standing_alone
						FROM = {
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = non_aggression_pact
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = guarantee
								active = yes
							}
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 365
							}
						}
						every_other_country = {
							limit = {
								is_neighbor_of = PREV
								is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = non_aggression_pact
								active = yes
							}
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 365
							}
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = fascism
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 60
							fascism = 40
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.313.a
		trigger = {
			is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			release_puppet = MEN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.313.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			give_guarantee = MEN
		}
	}
}

# Anti-Chiang War: War with Guangxi
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.314
	title = ww1_china.314.t
	desc = ww1_china.314.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		country_exists = GXC
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.314.a
		GXC = {
			clear_all_relations = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			set_country_flag = first_chiang_gui_war
			set_global_flag = first_chiang_gui_war
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = GZC
			}
			GZC = {
				clear_all_relations = yes
				get_current_government_type = yes
				GXC = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PREV
						autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					}
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = GXC
					enemy = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = ROOT
				enemy = GXC
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = ROOT
				enemy = GZC
			}
		}
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = { has_character = HNC_tang_shengzhi }
			HNC_tang_shengzhi = {
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_li_jishen }
			CHI_li_jishen = {
				set_character_flag = exiled
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = conservatism
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = stratocracy
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_china.315
				days = 45
			}
		}
	}
}

# Anti-Chiang War: Second War with Guangxi
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.316
	title = ww1_china.316.t
	desc = ww1_china.316.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
		has_global_flag = first_chiang_gui_war
		GXC = {
			exists = yes
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = first_chiang_gui_war
				has_country_flag = second_chiang_gui_war
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = second_chiang_gui_war
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 70
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.316.a
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = CHI_zhang_fakui
			}
			CHI_zhang_fakui = {
				set_nationality = GXC
			}
		}
		GXC = {
			clear_all_relations = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			set_country_flag = second_chiang_gui_war
			set_global_flag = second_chiang_gui_war
			CHI_zhang_fakui = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = warlordism
					}
					promote_character = warlordism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = warlordism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = conservatism
					}
					promote_character = conservatism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = conservatism
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Guangxijun"
					division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Guangxijun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.7	start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = ROOT
				enemy = GXC
			}
		}
	}
}

# Anti-Chiang War: War with Hunnan
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.317
	title = ww1_china.317.t
	desc = ww1_china.317.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.317.a
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = HNC_tang_shengzhi
			}
			HNC_tang_shengzhi = {
				set_nationality = HNC
			}
			GMJ_shi_yousan = {
				set_nationality = HNC
			}
		}
		HNC = {
			add_state_core = 602
			add_state_core = 893
			transfer_state = 602
			transfer_state = 893
			clear_all_relations = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			set_country_flag = chiang_tang_war
			set_global_flag = chiang_tang_war
			HNC_tang_shengzhi = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = conservatism
					}
					promote_character = conservatism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = conservatism
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Hunnanjun"
					division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						field_gun_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Hunnanjun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.7	start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = ROOT
				enemy = GXC
			}
		}
	}
}
